# D级生物类载具

<body>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">尸鬼蝙蝠</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">分类：坐骑</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：在一些圈子里被称为食尸鬼蝙蝠，尸鬼蝙蝠是被透肌魔人的邪恶妖术弄出的可憎的产物。透肌魔人专门用真菌和和人型生物的血肉来喂养魔宝蝙蝠。当它们成熟的时候，透肌魔人们会用腐败的毒素杀死它们，然后尸体复活成不死生物，作为坐骑和卫兵</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">分类</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">坐骑</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">最温顺最常见的怪物</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; <p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">生物类型</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">动物</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">体型</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">超</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">大</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">型生物</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">（特殊：食草龙的体积为</font><font face="宋体">20，是超大型生物，但是除了占据面积之外的其他体型调整值按照大型生物判定）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">专长</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">荒野求生</font>1</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，强健背肌</font><font face="宋体">1，死硬1，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">扫堂腿</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">2</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">武器伤害</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri">2</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">L的</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">伤害</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">防御</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">6</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">点天生防御</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，拥有黑暗视觉</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">甩尾</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">食草龙可以用标准动作甩动</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">尾巴</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">对触及</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">距离</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">内所有敌方目标各</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">进行一次近战肉搏攻击。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">头突</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">食草龙以冲锋攻击命中目标</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">时，可以无需动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">对攻击目标</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">追加一次</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">冲撞。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">逃亡</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">食草龙可以消耗一个迅捷动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">使其自身和骑乘者在</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">1</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">轮内免疫借机攻击。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">喂养</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">食草</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">头食草</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">龙每天需要吃掉</font>100</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">公斤</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">的草料</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">饮水</font>20升,至少睡眠4小时,如果食水睡眠不足,</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">食草</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">龙会无视除了进食、饮水和休息以外的任何命令。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">此外</font>,不要忘记清理排泄物</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">。食草龙的排泄物是优质的肥料</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">一次排泄产生的排泄物可以满足半亩地一个月的肥料需求。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===========================================================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">四足亚龙</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">本质</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">魔幻</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">本质</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">来源：龙与地下城</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">价格</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">D+</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">5</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">00</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">分类</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">坐骑</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">描述</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">四足亚龙与彩色龙、宝石龙和金属龙有远亲关系</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">在基本形态上与它们相似。它们足够聪明</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">能听懂语言</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">但自己却不会说话</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">它们是受食物和欲望驱使的任性动物。在野外</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">它们是挑食者</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">情绪多变</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">倾向于在捕杀猎物之前先玩弄猎物。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">在一些地区地域</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">四足亚龙是从蛋中培育出来的</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">用作飞行坐骑。这些驯化的四足亚龙忠诚于它们的骑手并舍身保护。然而</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">试图将野生四足亚龙驯服到并放上马鞍的努力是危险的</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">因为这些生物在将它们的妄想成为它们主人的骑手从高处扔下来之前</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">常常假装服从。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">==============================================================</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<td style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 138.5pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-left-alt: none; mso-border-top-alt: 0.5000pt solid windowtext; mso-border-right-alt: 0.5000pt solid windowtext; mso-border-bottom-alt: 0.5000pt solid windowtext" valign="top" width="184">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p> </o:p></span></p></td></tr></table>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">==============================================================</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">生物类型</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">龙</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">体型</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">大</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">型生物</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">（</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">体积</font>8</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">专长</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">警觉</font>2，爪牙之厉</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">2</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">攻击：武器伤害</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">3</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">L，破甲</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">3</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">的</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">爪和牙，造成挥砍伤害</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">防御：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">6</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">点天生防御</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">飞龙双翼</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：四足亚龙的基础移动速度提升</font><font face="宋体">3米；此外，四足亚龙获得飞行能力，飞行速度等同自身基础移动速度。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">极速</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">飞掠</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：在飞行状态下时，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">四足亚龙和其骑乘者</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">进行的攻击行为</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">不会引发借机攻击。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">多重攻击</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">四足亚龙</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">可以用一个标准动作进行</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">2</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">次近战肉搏攻击</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">；</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">且</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">四足亚龙</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">进行冲锋时</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">可以发动两次而非一次近战肉搏攻击</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，这</font><font face="宋体">2</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">次攻击全部获得冲锋的加值</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">。但是发动本能力时，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">四足亚龙</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">造成的最终伤害减半；并且这些攻击无法触发任何攻击后可以触发的效果。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">喂养四足亚龙</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">：四足亚龙体型巨大，每天需要进食超过</font>40KG肉类，任何种类的肉食均可，若四足亚龙未获得足够的食物，其生理系属性会承受3点内在减值，只有进食足够的食物后再进行一次长休息才可恢复；若连续7天没有获得足够的食物，</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">四足亚龙</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">将背叛主人飞往野外自谋生路。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===========================================================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">枭熊</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">本质：魔幻本质</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">来源：龙与地下城</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font><font face="宋体">D+500</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">分类：坐骑</font><font face="宋体">/动物伙伴</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：猫头鹰的尖叫在黑暗山谷与蛮荒森林中回响，响彻寂静的夜晚宣布着猎物的死亡。像熊一样的身躯批覆着厚实蓬松的羽毛，一双圆鼓鼓的大眼里清澈的瞳孔从它的脑袋往外疯狂地瞪着。</font>
<font face="宋体">学者们长久以来一直在争论枭熊的起源。最常见的理论是，一个疯狂的法师用一只巨猫头鹰和一只熊杂交，创造出第一个标本。然而，一些可敬的精灵则声称自己认识这些生物已有数千年，而且一些精类生物坚持认为这些动物一直都存在妖精荒野内。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">==============================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">基本能力：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">生理系属性：力量</font><font face="宋体">9  敏捷3  耐力7</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">心智系属性：智力</font><font face="宋体">1  感知3  决心1</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">互动系属性：风度</font><font face="宋体">1  操控1  沉着1</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">==============================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">专业：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p></td>
<td style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 138.5pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-left-alt: none; mso-border-top-alt: 0.5000pt solid windowtext; mso-border-right-alt: 0.5000pt solid windowtext; mso-border-bottom-alt: 0.5000pt solid windowtext" valign="top" width="184">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p> </o:p></span></p></td></tr></table>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">==============================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">生物类型：魔兽</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">体型：大型生物（体积</font><font face="宋体">8）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">专长：死硬</font><font face="宋体">2，爪牙之厉2</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">攻击：武器伤害</font><font face="宋体">2L，破甲3的喙和爪，喙造成穿刺伤害，爪造成挥砍伤害</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">防御：</font><font face="宋体">3点天生防御</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">熊类嗅觉：枭熊拥有灵敏嗅觉。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">猫头鹰视觉：枭熊拥有黑暗视觉。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">疯狂爪击：枭熊可以消耗一个标准动作，进行两次近战肉搏攻击。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">但是发动本能力时，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">枭熊</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">造成的最终伤害减半；并且这些攻击无法触发任何攻击后可以触发的效果。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">暴走凶禽：枭熊的肉搏攻击检定获得</font><font face="宋体">6DP内在加值和</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">2点附加成功</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">精通擒抱：枭熊的擒抱检定额外获得</font><font face="宋体">6DP内在加值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">喂养枭熊</font><font face="宋体">:一只枭熊每天需要吃掉一头羊羔或者等量的肉类,饮水6升,至少睡眠4小时,如果食水睡眠不足,枭熊会无视除了进食、饮水和休息以外的任何命令。此外,不要忘记清理排泄物。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
